Description

Customers wanted to integrate Twilio Android SDK using Hyperloop. But when they try to call disconnect function its showing error.

Steps to Reproduce:

1. Import attached project 2. Run in android device 3. Click on *Connect* button. Alert message will display when connected 4. Clicked on *disconnect* button 5. App will throw error

*Test Project/Code *

Link: https://www.dropbox.com/s/91uizz6dj3jluew/TwilioTestAndroid.zip?dl=1

  2. Hans Kn√∂chel 2018-02-19

   I tested this with Hyperloop 3.0.2 and it works fine *if* I remove the "onDisconnected" callback. For some reason that particular one is causing the "Cannot read property 'apiName' of null" error:
   
       function roomListener() {
       return new Room.Listener({
           onConnected : function(_room) {
               room = _room;
               alert('Connected');
           },
           onConnectFailure : function(room, e) {
               Ti.API.info('onConnectFailure ');
           },
           // Comment in the following and it will crash on "Disconnect" again
           // onDisconnected : function(_room, e) {
           //     Ti.API.info('onDisconnected ');
           // },
           onParticipantConnected : function(room, participant) {
   
           },
           onParticipantDisconnected : function(room, participant) {
           },
           onRecordingStarted : function(room) {
           },
           onRecordingStopped : function(room) {
               Ti.API.info('onRecordingStopped ');
           }
       });
   }
   
    
   I really cannot find anything special for that particular callback, so maybe it even was a side effect of the beta version? Looking at recent versions, the Twilio Android Voice SDK is still in beta.
    3. 

  3. Hans Kn√∂chel 2018-02-19

   After investigating this a bit further, it looks like Twilio changed the way of connecting and handling video views between the beta versions, so I am unable to reproduce this issue with newer versions of the SDK. It requires some rewrite of the used Hyperloop code, because some classes like "LocalMedia" are not used for creating audio- and video-tracks anymore.
    4. 

  4. Eric Merriman  2018-08-06

   Closing as "not our bug". If you disagree, please reopen.
    5.
